<p><a href = vnd.unilang:probably.html>Probably</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>ultimately</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">patriarchālis</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:patriarch.html>patriarch</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aal</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:patriarchaal.html>patriarchaal</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:patriarchaal.html>patriarchaler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">patriarchaalst</b>)
</p>
